<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:16pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:14pt" align=center><B>Notice of 2003 Annual Meeting of Shareholders</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:16pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:14pt" align=center><B>To be Held on December 4, 2003</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>NOTICE IS HEREBY GIVEN</B> that the 2003 Annual Meeting of Shareholders of Aberdeen Idaho Mining Company (the &quot;Company&quot;), will be held at 2:00 p.m. (PST), on December 4, 2003, at the Washington Mutual Building, Conference Room A located at 601 W. Main Avenue, Spokane, Washington 99201, to consider and act upon the following matters:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>1.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:72pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>To consider and vote upon the merger of the Company with and into its wholly-owned Nevada subsidiary;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; width:540pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>2.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:72pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>To elect five persons to the Board of Directors of the Corporation to serve for a one-year term or until his respective successor is elected and has qualified;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>3.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:72pt; width:504pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>To transact such other business as may properly come before the meeting or any adjournment thereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>The close of business on October 15, 2003 has been fixed as the record date for the determination of the Shareholders entitled to notice of, and to vote at, the Annual Meeting and at any postponements or adjournments thereof. &nbsp;Only Shareholders of record on the books of the Company at the close of business on October 15, 2003 shall be entitled to notice of, and to vote at, the meeting or any adjournment thereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>It is important that your shares be represented at the meeting whether or not you are personally able to attend. You are therefore urged to complete, date and sign the accompanying Proxy and mail it in the enclosed postage-paid envelope as promptly as possible. Your Proxy is revocable, either in writing or by voting in person at the Annual Meeting, at any time prior to its exercise.</P>

<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt" noshade size=1.333>
<A NAME="QuickMark"></A><P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>ABERDEEN IDAHO MINING COMPANY</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>601 W. Main Ave., Suite 1017</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>Spokane, WA 99201</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center>_________________________</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>PROXY STATEMENT</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center>Relating to</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center>Annual Meeting of Shareholders</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center>to be held on December 4, 2003</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center>_________________________</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>INTRODUCTION</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>This Proxy Statement is being furnished by the Board of Directors of Aberdeen Idaho Mining Company (the &quot;Company&quot;) to holders of shares of the Company's $0.10 par value Common Stock (the &quot;Common Stock&quot;) in connection with the solicitation by the Board of Directors of Proxies to be voted at the Annual Meeting of Shareholders of the Company to be held on December 4, 2003, and any adjournment or adjournments thereof (the &quot;Annual Meeting&quot;) for the purposes set forth in the accompanying Notice of Annual Meeting. This Proxy Statement is first being mailed to Shareholders on or about October 27, 2003.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Management is the beneficial owner or has the authority to vote 2,326,631 shares (approximately 23.6%) of the Company&#146;s outstanding Common Stock. &nbsp;It is management's intention to vote all of its shares in favor of each matter to be considered by the Shareholders.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>PURPOSES OF ANNUAL MEETING</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>Merger with Subsidiary </B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>At the Annual Meeting, Shareholders entitled to vote (see &quot;Voting at Annual Meeting&quot;) will be asked to consider and vote upon the merger of the Company with and into its wholly-owned Nevada subsidiary, Aberdeen Mining Company. If approved, the domicile of the Company will be changed from the State of Idaho to the State of Nevada (see &quot;Merger with Subsidiary&quot;). &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>Election of Directors</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>At the Annual Meeting, Shareholders will be asked to consider and to take action on the election of three members to the Board of Directors to serve for one-year terms or until their respective successors are elected and qualified (see &quot;Election of Directors&quot;).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>Other Business</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">To transact such other business as may properly come before the Annual Meeting or any postponements or adjournments thereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>As your vote is important, it is requested that you complete and sign the enclosed Proxy and mail it promptly in the return envelope provided. &nbsp;Shares cannot be voted at the meeting unless the owner is present to vote or is represented by Proxy.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=right>3</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:7.2pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:181.3pt; width:576pt; line-height:9.2pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:7.2pt" align=justify><B>VOTING AT ANNUAL MEETING</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:540pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>1.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>Record Date</B>. &nbsp;The Board of Directors of the Company has fixed the close of business on October 15, 2003, as the record date for the purpose of determining Shareholders of the Company entitled to notice of and to vote at the Annual Meeting. &nbsp;At the close of business on that date, the Company had 9,866,200 &nbsp;issued and outstanding shares of Common Stock. A majority of such shares will constitute a quorum for the transaction of business at the Annual Meeting. &nbsp;Proxies which are submitted but are not voted for or against (because of abstention, broker nonvotes or otherwise) will be treated as present for all matters considered at the meeting.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:540pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>2.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>Solicitation of Proxies.</B> &nbsp;The accompanying Proxy is solicited on behalf of the Board of Directors of the Company, and the cost of solicitation will be borne by the Company. &nbsp;Following the original mailing of the Proxies and soliciting materials, directors, officers and employees of the Company &nbsp;may, but do not presently intend, to solicit Proxies by mail, telephone, telegraph, or personal interviews. The Company may request brokers, custodians, nominees, and other record holders to forward copies of the Proxies and soliciting materials to persons for whom they hold shares of the Company and to request authority for the exercise of Proxies. &nbsp;In such cases, the Company will reimburse such holders for their reasonable expenses. &nbsp;The Company does not intend to utilize the services of an outside proxy solicitati
on firm.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:540pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>3.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>Revocation of Proxy.</B> &nbsp;Any Proxy delivered in the accompanying form may be revoked by the person executing the Proxy by written notice to that effect received by the Secretary of the Company at any time before the authority thereby granted is exercised, by execution of a Proxy bearing a later date presented at the meeting, or by attendance of such person at the Annual Meeting.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:540pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>4.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>How Proxies will be Voted.</B> &nbsp;Proxies received by the Board of Directors in the accompanying form will be voted at the Annual Meeting as specified therein by the person giving the Proxy. &nbsp;If no specification is made with respect to the matters to be voted upon at the meeting, the shares represented by such Proxy will be voted FOR the merger of the Company with and into its wholly&#150;owned Nevada subsidiary; and FOR the nominees to the Board of Directors in the election of Directors. </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>All shares represented by valid Proxy will be voted at the discretion of the proxy holders on any other matters that may properly come before the meeting. &nbsp;However, the Board of Directors does not know of any matters to be considered at the meeting other than those specified in the Notice of Meeting.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:36pt; text-indent:-36pt; width:540pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>5.</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>Voting Power.</B> &nbsp;Shareholders of the Common Stock of the Company are entitled to one vote for each share held. There is no cumulative voting for directors.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=right>4</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; width:540pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>Principal Shareholders.</B> &nbsp;The following table sets forth the identity of the record owners of more than five percent (5%) of the outstanding shares of any class of the Company as of &nbsp;October 15, 2003:</P>
