<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=right>13</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:576pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>Tax Aspects</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>It is management&#146;s belief that pursuant to the Internal Revenue Code Section 368 (a)(1)(F), this change of domicile from Idaho to Nevada will qualify as a tax free exchange as a mere change in identity, form or place of incorporation of one corporation, however effected. </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Assuming that the merger of the Company into its wholly-owned subsidiary qualifies as a reorganization within the meaning of Section 368(a) of the Code:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:18pt; text-indent:-18pt; width:543.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Symbol; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&bull;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:18pt; width:543.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Symbol; font-size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">No gain or loss will be recognized by a Shareholder of the Company as a result of the merger with respect to shares of the Company converted solely into shares of the surviving company;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:18pt; text-indent:-18pt; width:543.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Symbol; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&bull;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:18pt; width:543.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Symbol; font-size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The tax basis of the shares of stock of the surviving company received by the Company&#146;s Shareholders will be the same as the tax basis of the Company&#146;s stock exchanged therefor;</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; padding-left:18pt; text-indent:-18pt; width:543.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Symbol; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&bull;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:18pt; width:543.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Symbol; font-size:12pt" align=justify><FONT FACE="Times New Roman">The holding period of the surviving company stock received by the Company&#146;s Shareholders in the merger will include the period during which the Company&#146;s stock surrendered in exchange therefor were held, provided that such shares of the Company were held as capital assets at the effective date of the merger.</FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>No Opinion of Counsel and Advice to Seek Own Tax Adviser</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Neither the Company nor the nominees for Director have sought an opinion of counsel with respect to the tax consequences of the transactions to be considered at the meeting. The Company and the nominees do not believe that the reincorporation in Nevada will have any tax consequences to the Company's Shareholders. Shareholders are advised to consult with their own tax advisers or counsel if they have any questions regarding the tax aspects of the transaction.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>Board Recommendation </B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>The proposal to merge the Company with its wholly-owned Nevada subsidiary will require the affirmative vote of the holders of at least a majority of the shares entitled to vote thereon. The Board of Directors recommends a vote FOR the change of the Company&#146;s state of domicile from Idaho to Nevada. </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:-14pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>2. </B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>ELECTION OF DIRECTORS</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>At the meeting, five (5) Directors are to be elected who shall hold office until the next Annual Meeting of Shareholders and until their respective successors shall have been elected and qualified. There are no standing audit, nominating or compensation committees of the Board of Directors.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>The Proxies appointed in the accompanying Proxy intend to vote, unless directed to the contrary therein, in their discretion, for the election to the Board of Directors of the five persons named below, all of whom management believes are willing to serve the Company in such capacity. &nbsp;However, if any nominee at the time of election is unable or unwilling to serve, or is otherwise unavailable for election, such that substitute nominees are designated, the Proxies in their discretion intend to vote for all or a lesser number of such other nominees.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Martyn Alden Powell has been the President and a Director of the Company since February 2002. &nbsp;For the past fourteen years, Mr. Powell has been employed as a Realtor in the greater Seattle area. &nbsp;Since January 1999, Mr. Powell has been the President and a Director of Missouri River and Gold Gem Corporation, an inactive reporting public company founded by his father in 1983. &nbsp;Missouri River is currently seeking a business acquisition or merger but is not in negotiations with any entity with regard to a potential merger or acquisition. Mr. Powell is the owner of 1,317,358 shares of Missouri River which represents approximately 26.7% of that company&#146;s outstanding stock. &nbsp;Mr. Powell purchased 27,358 shares of the company&#146;s stock in 1987 for $0.16 per share. &nbsp;In that same year he was gifted 20,000 shares from his father. &n
bsp;In January 1999 Mr. Powell acquired 850,000 shares from the then president and controlling shareholder of the Company for $5.00 and was gifted an additional 120,000 shares from his father. &nbsp;In April 2001 Mr. Powell acquired 300,000 shares from the company at a price of $0.05 per share in a private placement pursuant to Rule 506 of Regulation D. &nbsp;The company is traded on the OTC Bulletin Board under the symbol MRGG. The stock is currently trading trading at approximately $.20 per share. Mr. Powell receives no compensation for serving in the capacity of President or Director of Missouri River Gold and Gem Corporation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>From June 2001 until October 1, 2003 Mr. Powell has served as Secretary and a Director of Quad Metals Corporation, an inactive reporting public company. &nbsp;Mr. Powell is the owner of 100,000 shares of Quad Metals (5.4%) for which he paid $5,000. &nbsp;The shares were purchased in September 2001 in private placement pursuant to Rule 506 of Regulation D. On October 1, 2003 Quad Metals completed a share exchange with DataJungle, LTD. Pursuant to the terms of the share exchange agreement, Quad Metals issued approximately 13,000,000 shares of common stock in exchange for all of the common stock of DataJungle and the conversion of certain outstanding DataJungle debt. &nbsp;DataJungle is a software company incorporated under the Canada Business Corporation Act, which develops and markets web-based, enterprise-class business intelligence software solutions t
hat translate business data into interactive tables, charts and maps. &nbsp;These solutions consist of modules of functionality that can be assembled to the specific requirements of the customer and customized to the needs of each user class within the customer's business. &nbsp;The company's software extends, and is complementary to, the products of most leading vendors of business intelligence software. DataJungle's software represents a new class of business intelligence applications that leverage XML Web Services and vector graphics based delivery formats, two of the emerging trends defining the direction of business applications &nbsp;Quad Metals is traded on the NASDAQ supervised OTC Bulletin Board. The stock was quoted at $1.01 as of the Close of business on October 6, 2003. Mr. Powell received no compensation for serving as an officer or director of Quad Metals. </P>

<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Robert William O&#146;Brien has been the Secretary/Treasurer and a Director of the Company since February 2002. Mr. O&#146;Brien graduated from Gonzaga University with a B.A. degree in Economics. Since July 1996, Mr. O&#146;Brien has been the sole owner and manager of Spokane Quotation Bureau, LLC, a company that publishes stock quotations for companies traded over-the-counter. Since June 2001 Mr. O&#146;Brien has served as President and a Director of Quad Metals Corporation, an inactive reporting public company. &nbsp;Mr. O&#146;Brien is the owner of 341,000 shares of Quad Metals, Inc. (18.85%) for which he paid $18,000. &nbsp;The shares were purchased in September 2001 in private placement pursuant to Rule 506 of Regulation D. (see the discussion of Mr. Powell&#146;s business experience above for a description of Quad Metals 
business activity). &nbsp;Mr. O&#146;Brien receives no compensation for serving as an officer or director of Quad Metals. Mr. O&#146;Brien served as the Secretary and a Director of Orbit E-Commerce, Inc., formerly New Hilarity, Inc. &nbsp;New Hilarity was incorporated under the laws of the State of Idaho on February 27, 1930 for the primary purpose of exploring and the development of mining properties. &nbsp;In 1993, the Company became an inactive mining company, and the Company thereupon decided to explore alternative business opportunities. &nbsp;In April 1999, the Company reorganized under the laws of the State of Nevada and changed its name from Lexington Mining Company to New Hilarity, Inc. and on April 12, 2001 changed its name again to Orbit E-Commerce, Inc. &nbsp;As of September 8, 2000, and pursuant to an Agreement and Plan of Reorganization dated as of August 3, 2000 by and between OECI and Orbit Canada Inc., an Ontario corporation (&quot;Orbit&quot;), OECI acquired Orbit as a result of which Orbit
 became a wholly-owned subsidiary of the Company (the &quot;Orbit Transaction&quot;). The Orbit Transaction resulted in a reverse take over, therefore, giving the stockholders of Orbit control of OECI. In connection with the Orbit Transaction, Mr. O&#146;Brien and the existing Board of Directors of the Company resigned and the directors of Orbit were appointed to the Board of the Company. Mr. O&#146;Brien received no compensation for serving as an officer or director of the company. The company is currently traded on the Over the Counter Bulletin Board under the Symbol &#147;OECI&#148;. Mr. O&#146;Brien served as a Director and Secretary/Treasurer of Gold Bond Resources, Inc. from March 2000, and additionally as the Chief Executive Officer of the company from November 2001, until the acquisition of EnerTeck, Chemical Corporation in January 2003. Mr. O&#146;Brien purchased 395,585 shares at $.005 per share in March of 2000, an additional 1,400,000 shares in October of 2000 at $.005 per share and an additional
 35,000 shares at $.10 per share in October of 2001. &nbsp;As of June 1, 2003, Mr. O&#146;Brien had approximately 1,700,000 shares remaining unsold. His sales were made at an average of $.35 per share. &nbsp;The stock is currently trading trading at approximately $.35 per share. Mr. O&#146;Brien received no compensation in connection as an officer or director of Gold Bond or in connection with the acquisition of EnerTeck Chemical Corporation. Mr. O&#146;Brien purchased 3.2 million shares of Daybreak Mines, Inc. at $.005 per share in December 2001. &nbsp;The stock currently trades at $.05. &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Dale Ben Lavigne has been a Director of the Company since January 1983. &nbsp;Mr. Lavigne has been a director of Daybreak Mining Company for more than 30 years and has served as Daybreak&#146;s President for more than 15 years. &nbsp;Daybreak is an inactive, reporting public company. &nbsp;Daybreak holds the mineral rights to approximately 340 acres in Shoshone County, Idaho. &nbsp;There are no known proven or probable ore reserves on the property. &nbsp;The company has not conducted active exploration activity on the property since approximately 1970 and the company is currently inactive. &nbsp;Mr. Lavigne is the owner of 743,425 shares of Daybreak common stock representing approximately 4.3% of the outstanding stock. &nbsp;Mr. Lavigne receives no compensation for serving as an officer or director of Daybreak. Mr. Lavigne&#146;s prior experience with s
hell companies is related to mineral exploration companies which became inactive. Mr. Lavigne was a director, but not a stockholder of Idaho Montana Silver Mines at the time controlling interest was sold in February 2000. The company is now called Grant Douglas Acquisition Corp. The stock has been reverse split 1:55. </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=right>16</P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>There is no current market for the stock. Mr. Lavigne received no compensation in connection with the acquisition of the company. Mr. Lavigne was a director but not a stockholder of Capitol Silver Mines Inc. Control of the Company was acquired by Internet Culinary in June 1999. The stock was subsequently reverse split 1:50. There is no current market for the stock. Mr. Lavigne received no compensation in &nbsp;connection with the acquisition of the company. &nbsp;&nbsp;Mr. Lavigne was a director of &nbsp;Princeton Mining Company. In May 2001 control of the company was acquired by Lifestyle Innovations. The stock was subsequently reverse split 1:7. Mr. Lavigne owned 10,400 shares of the company which he sold for an average price of $0.60 per share. The stock is currently traded at approximately $5.45 per share. Mr. Lavigne recei
ved no Compensation in connection with the acquisition of the company. Mr. Lavigne was a director of Silver Ramona. Control of the company was acquired by Achievement Tech Holding in May 2000. The stock has been reverse split 1:3.82. The stock is currently traded at approximately $0.03 per share. Mr. Lavigne has sold no shares of the company&#146;s stock and currently owns 22,849 shares of the company&#146;s stock. Mr. Lavigne received no compensation in connection with the acquisition of control of the company. &nbsp;Mr. Lavigne graduated from the University of Montana with a B.S. Degree in Pharmacy. &nbsp;For the past 47 years Mr. Lavigne has been the Chairman and a Director of the Osburn Drug Company, Inc., a 4-store chain of drug stores in North Idaho. Mr. Lavigne is also a Director and Officer of Metropolitan Mines, Inc., a reporting publicly-held, inactive mineral exploration company. &nbsp;Mr. Lavigne is the former Chairman of the First National Bank of North Idaho; a former member of the Gonzaga Univ
ersity Board of Regents; past President of the Silver Valley Economic Development Committee and a current member of the Governor's Task Force on Rural Idaho.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Dennis Michael O&#146;Brien, a Certified Public Accountant, has been a Director of the Company since May 1999. Mr. O&#146;Brien is graduated from Northern Illinois University with a B.S. degree in accounting. &nbsp;Since 1990 Mr. O&#146;Brien has been employed by the H.F. Magnuson Company in Wallace, Idaho as an accountant. Mr. O&#146;Brien&#146;s prior experience with shell companies is related to mineral exploration companies which subsequently became inactive. Mr. O&#146;Brien was a director, but not a stockholder of Idaho Montana Silver Mines at the time controlling interest was sold in February 2000. The company is now called Grant Douglas Acquisition Corp. The stock has been reverse split 1:55. There is no current market for the stock. Mr. O&#146;Brien received no compensation in connection with the acquisition of the company. Mr. O&#146;Brien was
 a director but not a stockholder of Capitol Silver Mines Inc. Control of the Company was acquired by Internet Culinary in June 1999. The stock was subsequently reverse split 1:50. There is no current market for the stock. Mr. O&#146;Brien received no compensation in &nbsp;connection with the acquisition of the company. &nbsp;&nbsp;Mr. O&#146;Brien was a director but not a stockholder of &nbsp;Princeton Mining Company. In May 2001 control of the company was acquired by Lifestyle Innovations. The stock was subsequently reverse split 1:7. The stock is currently traded at approximately $5.45 per share. Mr. O&#146;Brien received no Compensation in connection with the acquisition of the company but was paid $2,000 to remain as a director of the company for four months after the change of control.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>James Francis Etter is a Director of the Company. Mr. Etter is graduated from Gonzaga University. Mr. Etter has been retired for more than the past five years.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt"><B>Compensation of Directors and Officers</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>During the past three fiscal years, none of the officers or directors has received any compensation directly or indirectly for service to the Company in such positions. </P>

<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B>Board Committees</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:9pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>The Company does not have any standing audit or nominating or compensation committees. The entire board performs the functions of the Audit, Nominating and Compensation Committees. &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:9pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Martyn A. Powell, Robert W. O&#146;Brien, James F. Etter, Dale B. Lavigne and Dennis M. O&#146;Brien, comprising the entire Board of Directors, performs the functions of the Audit Committee, recommends a firm of independent certified public accountants to audit the annual financial statements, discusses with the auditors and approves in advance the scope of the audit, reviews with the independent auditors their independence, the financial statements and their audit report, reviews management's administration of the system of internal accounting controls, and reviews the Company's procedures relating to business ethics. The Company does not currently have a written audit committee charter. James F. Etter, Dale B. Lavigne and Dennis M. O&#146;Brien are deemed to be independent directors as that term is defined in Rule 4200(a)(14) of the NASD&#146;s listin
g standards.</P>

<DESCRIPTION>ABERDEEN IDAHO MINING CO SCHEDULE 14A
<TEXT>
<!doctype html public "-//IETF//DTD HTML//EN">
<HTML>
<HEAD>
<TITLE>Exhibit 2</TITLE>
<META NAME="author" CONTENT="BJR">
<META NAME="date" CONTENT="01/02/2004">
</HEAD>
<BODY style="line-height:12pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Exhibit 2.1</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>EXHIBIT I</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>PLAN OF MERGER</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>This Plan of Merger is made and entered into this 30th day of August, 2003, by and between Aberdeen Idaho Mining Company, an Idaho corporation (&quot;Aberdeen &nbsp;Idaho&quot;), and Aberdeen Mining Company, a Nevada corporation (&quot;Aberdeen &nbsp;Nevada&quot; or the &quot;Surviving Corporation&quot;).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:210.15pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>RECITALS</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>A. Aberdeen Idaho is a corporation organized and existing under the laws of the State of Idaho and has authorized capital stock consisting of 10,000,000 shares of $0.10 par value common stock, of which 9,866,200 shares are issued and outstanding, and held by approximately 560 shareholders of record. </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>B. Aberdeen Nevada is a corporation organized and existing under the laws of the State of Nevada and has authorized capital stock consisting of 300,000,000 shares of common stock with $0.001 par value, of which 100 shares are issued and outstanding, and held by Aberdeen Idaho and 10,000,000 shares of preferred stock with no stated value and $0.001 par value, of which no shares are issued and outstanding.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>C. The Boards of Directors of Aberdeen Idaho and Aberdeen Nevada, respectively, deem it advisable for Aberdeen Idaho to merge with and into Aberdeen Nevada.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the mutual covenants and agreements contained herein, Aberdeen Idaho and Aberdeen Nevada hereby agree to the following Plan of Merger:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>1. <I>Names of Constituent Corporations.</I> Aberdeen Idaho will merge with and into Aberdeen Nevada. Aberdeen Nevada will be the Surviving Corporation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>2. <I>Terms and Conditions of Merger.</I> The effective date of merger shall be the last date upon which the Articles of Merger are filed with the Secretary of State of the State of Idaho and the State of Nevada. Upon the effective date of the merger, the separate corporate existence of Aberdeen Idaho shall cease; title to all real estate and other property owned by Aberdeen Idaho or Aberdeen Nevada shall be vested in Aberdeen Nevada without reversion or impairment; and the Surviving Corporation shall have all liabilities of Aberdeen Idaho and Aberdeen Nevada. Any proceeding pending by or against Aberdeen Idaho or Aberdeen Nevada may be continued as if such merger did not occur, or the Surviving Corporation may be substituted in the proceeding for Aberdeen &nbsp;Idaho.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Each share of Aberdeen Idaho issued and outstanding immediately prior to the effective date shall automatically become one share of Aberdeen Nevada.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>3. <I>Governing Law.</I> The laws of the State of Nevada shall govern the Surviving Corporation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>4. <I>Name.</I> The name of the Surviving Corporation shall be Aberdeen Mining Company, a Nevada corporation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>5. <I>Registered Office.</I> The address of the registered office of the Surviving Corporation shall be 502 E. John Street, Room E, Carson City, NV 89706.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=right><BR></P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-left:36pt; width:486pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:5pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>6. <I>Accounting.</I> The assets and liabilities of Aberdeen Idaho and Aberdeen Nevada (collectively the &quot;Constituent Corporations&quot;) as of the effective date of the merger shall be taken up on the books of the Surviving Corporation at the amounts at which they are carried at that time on the respective books of the Constituent Corporations.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>7. <I>Articles of Incorporation.</I> The Articles of Incorporation of Aberdeen Nevada shall constitute the Articles of Incorporation of the Surviving Corporation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>8. <I>Bylaws.</I> The Bylaws of Aberdeen Nevada as of the effective date of the merger shall be the Bylaws of the Surviving Corporation until the same shall be altered or amended in accordance with the provisions thereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>9. <I>Directors.</I> The directors of Aberdeen Idaho as of the effective date of the merger shall be the directors of the Surviving Corporation until their respective successors are duly elected and qualified.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>10. <I>Manner and Basis of Converting Shares.</I> As of the effective date of the merger:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:72pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>(a) Each share of Aberdeen Idaho common stock issued and outstanding shall become one share of common stock of Aberdeen Nevada, the Surviving Corporation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:72pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>(b) The Surviving Corporation shall convert or exchange each share of Aberdeen Idaho common stock for one share of the common stock of the Surviving Corporation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:72pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>(c) Any shares of stock of Aberdeen Idaho in the treasury of Aberdeen Idaho on the effective date of the merger shall be surrendered to the Surviving Corporation for cancellation, and no shares of the Surviving Corporation shall be issued in respect thereof.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:72pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>(d) On the effective date of the merger, holders of certificates of common stock in Aberdeen Idaho may, but shall not be required to, surrender them to the Surviving Corporation, or its appointed agent, in such manner as the Surviving Corporation legally shall require. Upon receipt of such certificates, the Surviving Corporation shall issue in exchange therefor, at the shareholder&#146;s expense, a certificate of shares of common stock in the Surviving Corporation representing the number of shares of stock to which such holder shall be entitled as set forth above.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:72pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>(e) In addition, such shareholders shall be entitled to receive any dividends on such shares of common stock of the Surviving Corporation that may have been declared and paid between the effective date of the merger and the issuance to such shareholder of the certificate of such common stock.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>11. <I>Shareholder Approval.</I> This Plan of Merger shall be submitted to the shareholders of Aberdeen Idaho and Aberdeen Nevada for their approval in the manner provided under the applicable laws, at meetings to be held on or before October 31, 2003, or at other such time as the Boards of Directors of Aberdeen Idaho and Aberdeen Nevada shall agree. After approval by a vote of the holders of a majority of the Aberdeen Idaho shares entitled to vote thereon and the holders of the majority of the Aberdeen Nevada shares entitled to vote thereon, if any, of each voting group, and the approval by a vote of the holders of a majority of the Aberdeen Idaho shares entitled to vote thereon and the holders of a majority of the Aberdeen Nevada shares entitled to vote thereon, if any, of each voting group, Articles of Merger shall be filed as required under the laws of the States of Id
aho and Nevada.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=right><BR></P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>12. <I>Termination of Merger.</I> This merger may be abandoned at any time prior to the filing of Articles of Merger with the Secretary of State, upon a vote of a majority of the Board of Directors of both Aberdeen Idaho and Aberdeen Nevada. If the merger is terminated, there shall be no liability on the part of either Constituent Corporation, their respective Boards of Directors, or shareholders.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>13. <I>Counterparts.</I> This Plan of Merger may be executed in any number of counterparts, and all such counterparts and copies shall be and constitute an original instrument.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:36pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>IN WITNESS WHEREOF, this Plan of Merger has been adopted by the undersigned corporations as of this 30<SUP>th</SUP> day of August, 2003.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:-12pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Aberdeen Idaho Mining Company, an </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:216pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Aberdeen Mining Company., a </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:-12pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Idaho corporation </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:252pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Nevada corporation</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:90pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:522pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>

<BODY style="line-height:12pt; font-size:10pt; color:#000000">
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Exhibit 3.1</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>EXHIBIT II</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=center>ARTICLES OF INCORPORATION</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=center>OF</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=center>ABERDEEN MINING COMPANY</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>The undersigned hereby executes the following Articles of Incorporation for the purpose of forming a corporation under the provisions of the laws of the State of Nevada pursuant to NRS 79.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:210pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>ARTICLE I</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:222.05pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Name</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>The name of the corporation is Aberdeen Mining Company.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:208.35pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>ARTICLE II</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:217.9pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Purpose</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>The purpose of this corporation shall be to transact any and all lawful business for which corporations may be incorporated under the laws of the State of Nevada, in general, to have and exercise all the powers conferred by the laws of Nevada upon corporations and to do any and all things hereinbefore set forth to the same extent as natural persons might or could do.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:206.65pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>ARTICLE III</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:216.2pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Duration</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>This corporation shall be of perpetual duration.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:206.4pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>ARTICLE IV</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:183.1pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Authorized Capital Stock</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; line-height:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">The authorized capital stock of the corporation shall consist of two (2) classes of stock, designated as Common Stock and Preferred Stock.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>The total number of shares of Common Stock that the corporation will have authority to issue is three hundred million (300,000,000) shares. &nbsp;The shares shall have par value of $.001 per share. &nbsp;All of the Common Stock authorized herein shall have equal voting rights and powers without restrictions in preference.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>The total number of shares of Preferred Stock that the corporation will have authority to issue is ten million (10,000,000) shares. &nbsp;The Preferred Stock shall have no stated value and par value of $.001 per share. &nbsp;The Preferred Stock shall be entitled to preference over the Common Stock with respect to the distribution of assets of the corporation in the event of liquidation, dissolution, or winding-up of the corporation, whether voluntarily or involuntarily, or in the event of any other distribution of assets of the corporation among its stockholders for the purpose of winding-up its affairs. &nbsp;The authorized but unissued shares of Preferred Stock may be divided into and issued in designated series from time to time by one or more resolutions adopted by the Board of Directors. The Directors in their sole discretion shall have the power to determine the relative powers, p
references, and rights of each series of Preferred Stock.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=right><BR></P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:208.1pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>ARTICLE V</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:196.85pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Preemptive Rights</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Stockholders of this corporation will have no preemptive rights to acquire additional shares issued by the corporation, or any securities convertible into, or carrying or evidencing any rights or option to purchase, any such shares.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:206.4pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>ARTICLE VI</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:220.1pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Voting</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>The holders of any of the corporation's capital stock shall possess voting power for the election of directors and for all other purposes, subject to such limitations as may be imposed by law and by any provision of the Articles of Incorporation in the exercise of their voting power. &nbsp;Cumulative voting for the election of directors is hereby expressly prohibited. &nbsp;The holders of Common Stock shall be entitled to one vote for each share held. &nbsp;All of the Common Stock authorized herein shall have equal voting rights and powers without restrictions in preference. </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:204.75pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>ARTICLE VII</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:196.45pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Board of Directors</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>The initial Board of Directors of this corporation shall consist of one (1) director. &nbsp;The number of directors constituting the Board of Directors of this corporation may be increased or decreased from time to time in the manner specified in the Bylaws of this corporation; provided, however, that the number shall not be less than one (1) or more than eleven (11). &nbsp;All vacancies in the Board of Directors, including those caused by an increase in the number of directors, may be filled by a majority of the remaining directors, though less than a quorum.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:203.05pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>ARTICLE VIII</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:198.8pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Director Liability</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>A director of the corporation shall not be personally liable to the corporation or its stockholders for monetary damages for conduct as a director, except for liability of the director for (i) acts or omissions that involve intentional misconduct or a knowing violation of law by the director; (ii) conduct which violates Chapter 78.300 of the Nevada Revised Statutes, pertaining to unpermitted distributions to stockholders; or (iii) any transaction from which the director will personally receive a benefit in money, property, or services to which the director is not legally entitled. If the laws of the State of Nevada are amended to authorize corporate action further eliminating or limiting the personal liability of directors, then the liability of a director of the corporation shall be eliminated or limited to the fullest extent permitted thereunder, as so amended. Any repeal or modificat
ion of the foregoing paragraph by the stockholders of the corporation shall not adversely affect any right or protection of a director of the corporation existing at the time of such repeal or modification.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=right><BR></P>
<HR style="padding-top:7.2pt; padding-bottom:7.2pt" noshade size=1.333>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=center>ARTICLE IX</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=center>Indemnification</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>The corporation is authorized to indemnify, agree to indemnify or obligate itself to advance or reimburse expenses incurred by its Directors, Officers, employees or agents to the full extent of the laws of the State of Nevada as may now or hereafter exist.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=center>ARTICLE X</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=center>Bylaws</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Subject to the power of stockholders to amend or repeal, the Board of Directors of this corporation shall have the power to enact and amend such Bylaws defining the powers and duties of the officers of the corporation and providing for such other matters in relation to its affairs as they may deem necessary and convenient, provided the same are not out of harmony with the laws of the State of Nevada or these Articles of Incorporation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=center>ARTICLE XI</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=center>Action by Majority Consent of Stockholders</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>Any action required or permitted to be taken at a meeting of the stockholders may be taken without a meeting if, before or after the action, a written consent thereto is signed by stockholders holding at least a majority of the voting power, except that if a different proportion of voting power is required for such an action at a meeting, then that proportion of written consents is required.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=center>ARTICLE XII</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=center>Amendments</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify>The corporation reserves the right to amend, alter, change or repeal any provision contained in these Articles of Incorporation in the manner now or hereafter prescribed by statute, and all rights conferred on the stockholders herein are granted subject to this reservation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-right:50.4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; width:561.6pt; font-family:Times New Roman" align=justify><BR></P>
